The service we'll be using will be the same as what the A&M football players use, so we'll have wi-fi and cool stuff like that. We've looked at other options too, and it'll be much more expensive to fly. We would also miss too much school taking vans. Keith, our beloved advisor, writes  official excuse letters for everyone that will get your tests rescheduled and excused from class.
